        function getCookie(name) {
            if (name === "locationSessionCookie" && typeof UserContextService !== "undefined" && UserContextService.isTelesalesAgent()) {
                return UserContextService.getLocationSessionCookie();
            } else {
                var start = document.cookie.indexOf(name + "=");
                var len = start + name.length + 1;
                if ((!start) && (name != document.cookie.substring(0, name.length))) {
                    return null;
                }
                if (start == -1) return null;
                var end = document.cookie.indexOf(";", len);
                if (end == -1) end = document.cookie.length;
                return unescape(document.cookie.substring(len, end));
            }
        }
        <!--temp fix end-- >

    function loadComponentScript(id,src, async, defer, isScriptLoadedRef) {
      if (isScriptLoadedRef && !isScriptLoadedRef.value) {
        let script = document.createElement('script');
        script.src = src;
        script.async = async;
        script.defer = defer;
        var targetElement = document.getElementById(id);
        if (targetElement) {
            targetElement.parentNode.insertBefore(script, targetElement);
        }
        isScriptLoadedRef.value = true;
      }
    }
</script>
    
</div>

               var vulnarabilityFound= "false";
                   if(vulnarabilityFound.indexOf("true")!=-1){
                   	window.location.href = "/";
                   }
            </script>

            function updateLPChatConfigObjWithProfileUserData() {

                    var userUUID;
                    var isGuest = true;

                    if (dcCookieObject) {
                        userUUID = dcCookieObject && dcCookieObject.uuid ? dcCookieObject.uuid : null;
                        isGuest = dcCookieObject ? dcCookieObject.isGuest : true;
                        uuid = userUUID;
                    }
                    if (userUUID && !isGuest) {
                        if (typeof UserContextService != undefined && UserContextService.LANDROVER_PROFILE != undefined) {

                                entity: UserContextService.LANDROVER_PROFILE.ENTITY.DEMOGRAPHICS
                            };

                            .done(function (data) {
                                if (data && data.userDetails && data.userDetails.firstName && data.userDetails.firstName != null && data.userDetails.firstName != 'null') {
                                    firstName = data.userDetails.firstName;
                                }
                                if (data && data.userDetails && data.userDetails.lastName && data.userDetails.lastName != null && data.userDetails.lastName != 'null') {
                                    lastName = data.userDetails.lastName;
                                }
                                if (data && data.userDetails && data.userDetails.uuid && data.userDetails.uuid != null && data.userDetails.uuid != 'null') {
                                    uuid = data.userDetails.uuid;
                                }
                            });
                        }
                    }
                } catch (e) {
                    console.log('!! Some error occurred in updateLPChatConfigObjWithProfileUserData() !!');
                }
            }

            function setLPTagPage(eleSecId) {
                //var pagePath = '/content/aarpmedicareplans/en/health-plans/vpp-plan-details-header';
                var pageName = 'vpp-plan-details-header';
                var pageTitle = 'Plan Detail Header';
                if(pageTitle.includes('?')){
					pageTitle=pageTitle.replace(/\?/g, "");
                }else if(pageTitle.includes('&')){
                	pageTitle=pageTitle.replace(/\&/g, "and");
                }
                var sectionIdPage = '';
                if(location.href.indexOf('#MEDSUPP') > -1){
					sectionIdPage = 'health-plans:VPP MS Plans List';
                } else if (location.href.indexOf('/health-plans/medsupp-details.html') > -1){
                	sectionIdPage = 'health-plans:VPP MS Plans:Plan Details';
                } else if(location.href.indexOf('/health-plans/medsupp-plan-compare') > -1){
                	sectionIdPage = 'health-plans:VPP MS Plans:Plan Compare';
                } 
                else{
                    if (pageName === 'en' || pageName === 'homepage-classic' || pageName === 'homepage-4') {
                        sectionIdPage = 'HOME';
                        pageLanguage = 'English';
                    }
                    else if (pagePath) {
                        for (var i = 4; i <= pagePath.split('/').length - 2; i++) {
                            sectionIdPage += pagePath.split('/')[i] + ':';
                        }
                        sectionIdPage += pageTitle;
                    }
                }   
                
                setTimeout(function () {
                    //var lpPsc = (typeof getLatestPSC != "undefined") ? getLatestPSC() : "";
                    var lpPsc = null;
                    var TFNSessionCookieVar = getCookie('TFNSessionCookie');
                    if (TFNSessionCookieVar != null && typeof(TFNSessionCookieVar) != 'undefined') {
                        var values = TFNSessionCookieVar.split(',');
                        if (values[0] != null) {
                        lpPsc = values[0];
                        }
                    }
                    var lpReferringURL = window.location.href.split("?")[0];
                    var lpAdobeID = "";
                    if (typeof _satellite !== 'undefined') {
                    var lpAdobeID = _satellite.getVar("mcid");
                    }
                    var dynatraceVisitorId = "";
                    if (typeof dynatrace != "undefined" && typeof dynatrace.getVisitorID != "undefined") {
                    dynatraceVisitorId = dynatrace.getVisitorID();
                    }
                    console.log("psc {}" + lpPsc);
                    if(typeof lpTag !== 'undefined' && lpTag) {
                        lpTag.sdes = lpTag.sdes || [];
                        lpTag.sdes.push([{
                            "type": "ctmrinfo",
                            "info": {
                            "customerId": "Shopper profile UUID:"+uuid,
                            "socialId": "RX Visitor ID:"+dynatraceVisitorId,
                            "imei": "Adobe ID:"+lpAdobeID,
                            "userName":firstName+lastName
                            }
                        },
                        {
                            "type": "mrktInfo",
                            "info": {
                            "campaignId": lpPsc
                            }
                        }
                        ]);
                    }
                }, 3000);
                lpTag.events.bind("LP_OFFERS", "OFFER_DISPLAY", offerDisplay);
                lpTag.events.bind("LP_OFFERS", "OFFER_CLICK", offerClick); 
                lpTag.events.bind("lpUnifiedWindow", "state", function (data, info) {
                    if (data.state === 'init') {
                        initButtons('init');
                    }

                    if (data.state === 'interactive') {
                        if (typeof _satellite !== 'undefined')  {
                            _satellite.track('preChatWindowChatButtonClicked');
                        }
                        initButtons('interactive');
                        if(typeof customTracking !=='undefined'){
                            customTracking.startCustomTrackingV2(customTracking.infoType.USER_ACTION,(location.hostname.indexOf("aarpmedicareplans")> -1 ? "AMP" : "UMS")+' # Chat conversation initiated','',customTracking.eventType.ACTION);
                        }
                    }
                });
                console.log("==> in liveperson", lpTag);

                if (location.href.includes("/plan-recommendation-engine.html")) {
    			sectionIdPage = 'PRE:';
    			eleSecId = location.pathname.split("plan-recommendation-engine.html/")[1] || '';
		}

                if (lpTag) {
                    var finaleleSecId = 'SEC-' + lpSectionSiteId + ':' + pageLanguage + ':' + sectionIdPage + (eleSecId ? eleSecId : '');
                    if (location.pathname === '/health-plans/plan-summary' || location.pathname + location.hash === '/health-plans/plan-summary/#MA'
                        || location.pathname + location.hash === '/health-plans/plan-summary/#PDP' || location.pathname + location.hash === '/health-plans/plan-summary/#SNP') {
                        sectionIdPage = 'health-plans:VPP Plan summary';
                        console.log('section id {}', 'SEC-' + lpSectionSiteId + ':' + pageLanguage + ':' + sectionIdPage);
                        lpTag.section = ['SEC-' + lpSectionSiteId + ':' + pageLanguage + ':' + sectionIdPage];
                    } else if (location.pathname === '/medicare/health-plans/plan-summary' || location.pathname + location.hash === '/medicare/health-plans/plan-summary/#MA'

            function offerDisplay(data, info) {            
                //$('#amp_message_button .uhc-tfn').attr('tabindex', '0'); // SAM re active Chat button recive focus
                if (data.engagementName.includes('- Pro')) {
                    if (typeof _satellite !== 'undefined')  {
                        _satellite.track('proactiveChatOffered');
                    }
                }
                $('#amp_message_button .uhc-tfn').on("keydown", function (e) { // SAM Chat Now Button Keydown event for WCAG tab and Shift Tab keys
                    var code = e.keyCode ? e.keyCode : e.which;
                    if (e.shiftKey && code == 9) {
                        $('.saved_items_container .mySavedItem').focus();
                        e.preventDefault();
                    } else if (!e.shiftKey && code == 9) {
                        $('#sam-call-button').focus();
                        e.preventDefault();
                    } else if (!e.shiftKey && code == 32) {
                        $(this).trigger('click');
                        e.preventDefault();
                    }
                });

                $(".proactive-chat-cross").off("click").on("click", function () { // for "  2	Proactive chat 	X " from Excel
                    if (typeof _satellite !== 'undefined')  {
                    _satellite.track('proactiveNo');
                    }
                });

                if(data && data.engagementName && data.engagementName.includes("Inline Reactive")){
                    console.log("inside if cta reactive {}",data.engagementName);
                    $('#chatOnHrs').show();
                    $('#chatOffHrs').hide();
                    $('.chatNowBtn a').attr('tabindex','0');
                }
            }

            function offerClick(data, info) {
                if(data && data.engagementName){
                    if (data.engagementName.includes('- Pro') || data.engagementName && data.engagementName.includes('- PRO')) {
                        if (typeof _satellite !== 'undefined')  {
                            _satellite.track('proactiveYes');
                            _satellite.track('chatEngagementId', {
                            engId : data.engagementId ? data.engagementId:'',
                            btnName : 'Proactive Chat'
                        });
                        }
                        if(typeof customTracking !=='undefined'){
                            customTracking.startCustomTrackingV2(customTracking.infoType.USER_ACTION,(location.hostname.indexOf("aarpmedicareplans")> -1 ? "AMP" : "UMS")+' # Proactive Chat Button Clicked','',customTracking.eventType.ACTION);
                        }
                    } else if (data.engagementName.includes('- Reactive')) {
                        if (typeof _satellite !== 'undefined')  {
                            _satellite.track('reactiveChatButtonClicked');
                            _satellite.track('chatEngagementId', {
                                engId : data.engagementId ? data.engagementId:'',
                                btnName : 'Reactive Chat'
                            });
                        }
                        if(typeof customTracking !=='undefined'){
                            customTracking.startCustomTrackingV2(customTracking.infoType.USER_ACTION,(location.hostname.indexOf("aarpmedicareplans")> -1 ? "AMP" : "UMS")+' # Reactive Chat Button Clicked','',customTracking.eventType.ACTION);
                        }
                    }else if (data.engagementName.includes('Inline Reactive')) {
                        var dataStore = {
                            "engId" : data.engagementId ? data.engagementId:'',
                            "btnName" : 'CTA Chat now',
                            "event": "linkClick",
                            "assetid": createUUID(),
                            "assetContainer": "Chat with UnitedHealthcare",
                            "assetName": "Chat now",
                            "eventDetail": "linkClick"
                        };
                        appEventData.push(dataStore);
                    }
                }
            }

            function initButtons(state) {
                // 3 Dots Menu Clicked
                $(".lp_menu-top-btn").off("click").on("click", function () {
                    // End Conversation
                    $(".lp_top_close_action").off("click").on("click", function () {
                    // If Yes and No button are presented (IN CONVERSATION)
                    if ($(".lpc_confirmation-dialog__confirm-button").length) {
                        $(".lpc_confirmation-dialog__confirm-button")
                        .off("click")
                        .on("click", function () {
                            if (typeof _satellite !== 'undefined')  {
                                _satellite.track('endConversationYes');
                            }
                        });

                        $(".lpc_confirmation-dialog__cancel-button")
                        .off("click")
                        .on("click", function () {
                            if (typeof _satellite !== 'undefined')  {
                                _satellite.track('endConversationNo');
                            }
                        });
                        // If Yes and No do not exist (No Chat Initiated)
                        } else {
                            if (state == "init") {
                                if (typeof _satellite !== 'undefined')  {
                                    _satellite.track('endConversation');
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        if (state == "interactive") {
                            if (typeof _satellite !== 'undefined')  {
                            _satellite.track('endConversation');
                            }
                        }
                    });

                    // Print Conversation
                    $("button[aria-label='Print transcript'").off("click").on("click", function () {
                        if (typeof _satellite !== 'undefined')  {
                            _satellite.track('printTranscript');
                        }
                    })
                });
            }
        </script>

                                              <span class="sr-only">footnote</span>
                                              <div id="planSummaryFootNotesDiv" class="footnotes ng-scope footnotesblock"><h6 style="font-size: inherit; font-weight: inherit; color: rgb(0,38,119);"><b style="color: inherit; font-size: inherit;">Disclaimer information</b></h6>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"></span></p>
                          <p><b>Enrollment Disclaimer Information:</b></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph">Plans are insured through UnitedHealthcare Insurance Company or one of its affiliated companies, a Medicare Advantage organization with a Medicare contract and a Medicare-approved Part D sponsor. Enrollment in these plans depends on the plans contract renewal with Medicare. UnitedHealthcare Insurance Company paid royalty fees to AARP for the use of its intellectual property. These fees are used for the general purposes of AARP. AARP and its affiliates are not insurers. You do not need to be an AARP member to enroll. AARP encourages you to consider your needs when selecting products and does not make specific product or pharmacy recommendations for individuals. UnitedHealthcare contracts directly with Walgreens for this plan; AARP and its affiliates are not parties to that contractual relationship.</span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"></span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"><b>Extra Help:</b><br>
                          </span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph">If you receive Extra Help from Medicare, your copays may be lower or you may have no copays.</span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"></span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"><b>Featured Benefits:</b></span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph">- Benefits, features and/or devices vary by plan/area. Limitations, exclusions and/or network restrictions may apply.</span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"></span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph">-Other hearing exam providers are available in the UnitedHealthcare network. The plan only covers hearing aids from a UnitedHealthcare Hearing network provider.</span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"></span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph">-For Chronic Special Needs Plans - You will pay a maximum of $25 for each 1-month supply of Part D covered insulin drug through all coverage stages, except the Catastrophic drug payment stage where you pay $0.</span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"></span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph">-For All Other Plans - You will pay a maximum of $35 for each 1-month supply of Part D covered insulin drug through all coverage stages, except the Catastrophic drug payment stage where you pay $0.</span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"></span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph">-Food, OTC and utility benefits have expiration timeframes. Call your plan or review your Evidence of Coverage (EOC) for more information.</span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"></span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph">- Eligibility for the healthy food and utilities benefit under the Value-Based Insurance Design model is limited to members with Extra Help from Medicare and will be determined after enrollment.</span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"></span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph">- For C-SNP: The healthy food benefit is a special supplemental benefit only available to chronically ill enrollees with a qualifying condition, such as diabetes, chronic heart failure and/or cardiovascular disorders, and who also meet all applicable plan coverage criteria. Contact us for details.</span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"></span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph">- For D-SNP, TN only: The healthy food benefit is a special supplemental benefit only available to chronically ill enrollees with a qualifying condition, such as high blood pressure, high cholesterol, chronic and disabling mental health conditions, diabetes and/or cardiovascular disorders, and who also meet all applicable plan coverage criteria. There may be other qualified conditions not listed. Contact us for details.</span></p>
                          <p></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph">-The fitness benefit includes a standard fitness membership. The information provided is for informational purposes only and is not medical advice. Consult your doctor prior to beginning an exercise program or making changes to your lifestyle or health care routine. Gym network may vary in local market and plan.</span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"></span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph">-If your plan offers out-of-network dental coverage and you see an out-of-network dentist, you might be billed more. Network size varies by local market.</span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"></span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph">-Routine transportation not for use in emergencies.</span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"></span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph">-Virtual visits may require video-enabled smartphone or other device. Not for use in emergencies. Not all network providers offer virtual care.</span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"></span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph">- $0 copays may be restricted to preferred home delivery prescriptions during the initial coverage phase and may not apply during the Catastrophic stage. Optum Home Delivery Pharmacy and Optum Rx are affiliates of the UnitedHealthcare Insurance Company. You are not required to use Optum Home Delivery Pharmacy for medications you take regularly. There may be other pharmacies in your network.</span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"></span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"></span></p>
                          <p><b>The Medicare Prescription Payment Plan:</b><br>
                          </p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph">Starting Jan. 1, 2025, if you spend more than $2,000 for covered Part D prescription drugs each year, you may want to participate in the Medicare Prescription Payment Plan. This payment plan spreads your out-of-pocket prescription drug costs over the remainder of the calendar year. Learn more about the <a title="Medicare Prescription Payment Plan" class="rte_link_InText" href="/medicare/medicare-education/prescription-payment-plan.html" target="_blank">Medicare Prescription Payment Plan</a>.<br>
                           </span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"><b>Out-of-network:</b><br>
                          </span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph">Out-of-network/non-contracted providers are under no obligation to treat members, except in emergency situations. Please call our customer service number or see your Evidence of Coverage for more information, including the cost-sharing that applies to out-of-network services.</span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"></span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"><b>State-Level Medicaid,D-SNP Disclaimer:<br>
                          </b></span></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph">D-SNP and C-SNP:The values shown in-network represent a range based upon the amount of the Medicare Parts A and B plan cost sharing covered by the state. Depending on your Medicaid eligibility, your Medicaid program may have cost sharing. For complete information, and for costs for those without Medicare Parts A and B plan cost sharing covered by the state, and applicable Medicaid cost sharing, please refer to your Summary of Benefits or Evidence of Coverage. Limitations, exclusions, and restrictions may apply.</span></p>
                          <p></p>
                          <p><span class="paragraph"><b>Other Languages:</b><br>
                          </span></p>

    <div data-cmp-is="image" data-cmp-src="/content/experience-fragments/acquisition-global-xf/chat-cta/chat-cta/chat-cta-and-call/_jcr_content/root/layout_container/content/layout_container_137/content/image_copy.coreimg{.width}.png/1727265859245/chatbubble-illustration-rgb.png" data-asset-id="7a499181-82cb-47da-a799-30234db76c42" id="image-69e446148a" data-cmp-hook-image="imageV3" class="cmp-image" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject">
        
            <img src="/medicare/content/experience-fragments/acquisition-global-xf/chat-cta/chat-cta/chat-cta-and-call/_jcr_content/root/layout_container/content/layout_container_137/content/image_copy.coreimg.png/1727265859245/chatbubble-illustration-rgb.png" loading="lazy" fetchpriority="low" decoding="async" class="cmp-image__image" itemprop="contentUrl" width="300" height="225" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" alt>

    <script defer>
        // Use an event listener with passive option for better performance
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            // Get all images that need srcset manipulation
            const imagesToManipulate = document.querySelectorAll('img[data-custom-srcset].cmp-image__image');
            
            // Skip processing if no images found
            if (!imagesToManipulate.length) return;
            
            const path = window.location.pathname;
            const host = window.location.host;
            const hostname = window.location.hostname;
            
            // Check path conditions once instead of for each image
            const isMedicarePath = path.startsWith("/medicare") || path.startsWith("/medicare/") || 
                                  path.startsWith("/medicare/medicare-education/");
            const isAARPorUHC = host.indexOf('aarpmedicareplans') > -1 || 
                               hostname.indexOf('uhcmedicaresolutions') > -1;
            
            if (isMedicarePath && !(host.indexOf('aarpmedicareplans') > -1)) {
                // Process all images at once with the medicare path prefix
                imagesToManipulate.forEach(function(image) {
                    const customSrcsetValue = image.getAttribute('data-custom-srcset');
                    if (!customSrcsetValue) return;
                    
                    const srcSetParts = customSrcsetValue.split(',').map(function(src) {
                        const parts = src.trim().split(' ');
                        return '/medicare' + parts[0] + ' ' + parts[1];
                    });
                    
                    image.setAttribute('srcset', srcSetParts.join(', '));
                    image.removeAttribute('data-custom-srcset');
                });
            } else if (isAARPorUHC) {
                // For AARP or UHC sites, just copy the custom srcset value
                imagesToManipulate.forEach(function(image) {
                    const customSrcsetValue = image.getAttribute('data-custom-srcset');
                    if (customSrcsetValue) {
                        image.setAttribute('srcset', customSrcsetValue);
                        image.removeAttribute('data-custom-srcset');
                    }
                });
            }
        }, {passive: true});
            // Apply lazy loading to images in XFs that may be added dynamically
            function applyLazyLoadingToXfImages() {
                var xfContainers = document.querySelectorAll('.xf-content-height, [class*="xf-container"]');
                xfContainers.forEach(function(container) {
                    var images = container.querySelectorAll('img:not([loading])');
                    images.forEach(function(img) {
                        if (!img.hasAttribute('data-no-lazy')) {
                            img.setAttribute('loading', 'lazy');
                            img.setAttribute('fetchpriority', 'low');
                            img.setAttribute('decoding', 'async');
                        }
                    });
                });
            }
    
            // Initial application
            applyLazyLoadingToXfImages();
    
            // Listen for XF content refreshes
            window.addEventListener('refreshXfContent', function() {
                setTimeout(applyLazyLoadingToXfImages, 100);
            });
    </script>
    </div>

<script>

    const AICompanionUtils = {

        CONTEXT_CONSTANTS: [
            {
                context: "VPP_PLAN_SUMMARY",
                regex: /\/health-plans\/plan-summary\//,
            },
            {
                context: "VPP_PLAN_DETAILS",
                regex: /\/health-plans\/details.html\//,
            },
            {
                context: "VPP_PLAN_COMPARE",
                regex: /\/health-plans\/plan-compare\//,
            },
            {
                context: "DEFAULT",
                regex: /^\/.*$/,
            },
        ],
        AI_COMPANION_ENABLED_LIST: [
            'VPP_PLAN_COMPARE',
            'VPP_PLAN_DETAILS',
            'VPP_PLAN_SUMMARY'
        ],
        AI_COMPANION_URL: '/ai-companion/index',
        // PRT - start
        PRT_COPILOT_URL: "/prt-copilot",
        PRT_COMPANION_ENABLED_LIST: ["VPP_PLAN_DETAILS"],
        // PRT - end
        getResolvedContext() {
            const url = window.location.pathname;
            for (const contextObj of this.CONTEXT_CONSTANTS) {
                const { context, regex } = contextObj;
                if (regex.test(url)) {
                    return context;
                }
            }
            return null;
        },

        isVPP(){
            const vppContext = this.getResolvedContext();
            return this.AI_COMPANION_ENABLED_LIST.includes(vppContext);
        },

        isDesktop(){
            return window.innerWidth > 1024;
        },
        getFlagSmithConfig(featureToggleName){
            if (typeof AICompanionContextService !== 'undefined' && AICompanionContextService.FEATURE_FLAGS) {
                return AICompanionContextService.FEATURE_FLAGS[featureToggleName] || { enabled: false, value: null };
            }
            return { enabled: false, value: null };  
        },
        getUserTypeBasedOnConfig(){
            const aiCompanionFeatureFlag = this.getFlagSmithConfig('feature_f1360943_ai_companion_enabled') || {};
            const value = aiCompanionFeatureFlag.value;

            if (aiCompanionFeatureFlag.enabled && value) {
                const agentList = value.toUpperCase().split(',');
                const agentProfileData = this.getAgentProfileData();

                if(agentProfileData){
                    const agentId = agentProfileData.salesforceData && agentProfileData.salesforceData.agentId;
                    return agentId && agentList.indexOf(agentId.toUpperCase()) > -1 ? "agent" : null;    
                } else if (agentList.indexOf('CONSUMER_AI_ENABLED') > -1) {
                    return "consumer";
                }
            }
            return null;
        },
        isPRTEnabled() {    
            const planCompanionFlagsmith = this.getFlagSmithConfig('feature_plan_companion_enabled') || {};
            const planCompanionData = this.parseJsonData(planCompanionFlagsmith.value);
            this.setLocalStorageItem("pdfHighlightText", (planCompanionData && planCompanionData.isHighlightText) || false);
            this.setLocalStorageItem("audioSupport", (planCompanionData && planCompanionData.isAudioSupport) || false);

            const agentProfileData = this.getAgentProfileData();

            if(agentProfileData && agentProfileData.salesforceData && agentProfileData.salesforceData.agentId){
                return false;
            }

            const countyInfo = document.planData ? document.planData.countyInfo || document.planData.selectedCounty : null;
            const planContextData = this.getContextData();
            const planType = planContextData && planContextData.planType;

            var isPlanCompanionEnabled = planCompanionFlagsmith.enabled;
            const countyDetails = planCompanionData && planCompanionData.countyDetails;

            if(!isPlanCompanionEnabled || 
               (planCompanionData.pages && planCompanionData.pages.indexOf(this.getResolvedContext()) < 0) ||
               (planCompanionData.ignorePlanTypes && (typeof planType != 'string' || planCompanionData.ignorePlanTypes.indexOf(planType.toUpperCase()) > -1)) ||
               (countyDetails && countyDetails.length > 0 && (!countyInfo || !countyInfo.fipsCountyName))){
               return false;
            }

            if(countyDetails && countyDetails.length > 0){
              isPlanCompanionEnabled = false;

              for (var i = 0; i < countyDetails.length; i++) {
                var countyDetail = countyDetails[i];
                
                if(countyDetail.county == countyInfo.fipsCountyCode && countyDetail.countyName && countyDetail.countyName.toUpperCase() == countyInfo.fipsCountyName.toUpperCase()){
                    isPlanCompanionEnabled = true;
                    if(!countyDetail.zipCodes || countyDetail.zipCodes.length == 0){
                        break;
                    }
                }
                if(!isPlanCompanionEnabled){
                    continue;
                }
                isPlanCompanionEnabled = false;

                if(countyDetail.zipCodes && countyDetail.zipCodes.indexOf(countyInfo.zipCode) > -1){
                    isPlanCompanionEnabled = true;
                    break;
                }
              } 
            }

            return isPlanCompanionEnabled;
        },
        getAgentProfileData() {
            try{
                if(typeof LANDROVER_UTILITY !== 'undefined' && typeof LANDROVER_UTILITY.getItem_SS == 'function'){
                    return JSON.parse(LANDROVER_UTILITY.getItem_SS(LANDROVER_UTILITY.AGENT_PROFILE_DATA));
                }
                return null;
            }catch(error){
                return null;
            }
        },
        parseJsonData(data) {
            if(!data){
                return null;
            }

            try{
                return JSON.parse(data);
            }catch(e){
                return null;
            }
        },
        setLocalStorageItem(key, value) {
            try{
                if(typeof globalCommonUtilityService !== 'undefined' && typeof globalCommonUtilityService.setValueInStorage == 'function'){
                    globalCommonUtilityService.setValueInStorage(globalCommonUtilityService.storageTypes.LOCALSTORAGE, key, value);
                }
            }catch(error){}
        },
        getContextData() {
            if (typeof AICompanionContextService !== 'undefined' && typeof AICompanionContextService.buildContextData == 'function') {
                return AICompanionContextService.buildContextData() || null;
            }

            return null;
        },
        isDisplayAICompanion() {
            return this.isVPP() && typeof getSiteId == 'function' && getSiteId() === 'AMP';
        },
        getSessionTrackingData(){
            if (typeof AICompanionContextService !== 'undefined' && typeof AICompanionContextService.getSessionTrackingData == 'function') {
                return AICompanionContextService.getSessionTrackingData() || {};
            }
            return {};
        }
    }
</script>


    <script type="text/javascript">
    (function () {
        try { 
        const prodUrls = [
            "https://green.prod-azure-aarpmedicareplans.uhc.com",
            "https://green.aarpmedicareplans.com",
            "https://preview.prod-azure-aarpmedicareplans.uhc.com",
            "https://preview.aarpmedicareplans.com",
            "https://www.prod-azure-aarpmedicareplans.uhc.com",
            "https://www.aarpmedicareplans.com",
            "https://green.prod-azure-uhcmedicaresolutions.uhc.com",
            "https://uhc-gpd-green.uhc.com",
            "https://preview.prod-azure-uhcmedicaresolutions.uhc.com",
            "https://www.prod-azure-uhcmedicaresolutions.uhc.com",
            "https://www.uhc.com"
       ];
        const isProd = prodUrls.includes(window.location.origin);
        const isAMS = window.location.origin.includes('aarpmedicareplans');
        
        console.log('[RvoHealth] Environment:', { env: window.location.origin, isProd, isAMS });

        function waitForFlagsmith(timeout) {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                const startTime = Date.now();
                const checkFlagsmith = () => {
                    try {
                        const flagsmithData = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('BULLET_TRAIN_DB') || '{}');
                        if (flagsmithData?.flags) {
                            console.log('[RvoHealth] Flagsmith data loaded successfully');
                            resolve(flagsmithData.flags);
                            return;
                        }
                    } catch (error) {
                        console.log('[RvoHealth] Error checking Flagsmith:', error);
                    }
                    
                    if (Date.now() - startTime > timeout) {
                        console.log('[RvoHealth] Flagsmith load timeout exceeded. Proceeding with defaults.');
                        resolve({});
                        return;
                    }
                    setTimeout(checkFlagsmith, 100);
                };
                checkFlagsmith();
            });
        }

        function getFlagSmithConfig(featureToggleName, flagsmithFlags) {
            try {
                if (flagsmithFlags && flagsmithFlags[featureToggleName]) {
                    return flagsmithFlags[featureToggleName];
                }
            } catch (error) {
                console.log('[RvoHealth] Error retrieving flag:', featureToggleName, error);
                return { enabled: false, value: null };
            }
            console.log('[RvoHealth] Flag not found:', featureToggleName, '- using default');
            return { enabled: false, value: null };
        }

        async function initRvoHealth() {
            const flagsmithFlags = await waitForFlagsmith(3000);
            
            const rvohConsumerFlag = getFlagSmithConfig('mavericks_rvoh_consumer_enabled', flagsmithFlags);
            const isRvohConsumerEnabled = rvohConsumerFlag.enabled === true;
            const telesalesFlag = getFlagSmithConfig('mavericks_rvoh_telesales_enabled', flagsmithFlags);
            const isRvohTelesalesEnabled = telesalesFlag.enabled === true;
            
            let rvohConfig = {};
            try {
                if (rvohConsumerFlag.value) {
                    rvohConfig = JSON.parse(rvohConsumerFlag.value);
                }
            } catch (error) {
                console.error('[RvoHealth] Error parsing flag value:', error);
            }
            
            const agentData = JSON.parse(sessionStorage.getItem('ucp_agentProfileData') || '{}');
            const isAgent = !!agentData?.agentFlow;
            const agentId = agentData?.salesforceData?.agentId || '';
            const telesalesAgentsList = telesalesFlag.value ? telesalesFlag.value.toUpperCase().split(',') : [];
            const isAgentAllowed = agentId && telesalesAgentsList.includes(agentId.toUpperCase());
            
            console.log('[RvoHealth] Configuration:', { 
                consumerEnabled: isRvohConsumerEnabled,
                telesalesEnabled: isRvohTelesalesEnabled,
                isAgent,
                agentId,
                isAgentAllowed
            });

            const keys = {
                writeKey: '',
                sourceKey: ''
            };
            
            if (rvohConfig.keys && rvohConfig.keys[isAMS ? 'ams' : 'uhcm']) {
                const envKeys = rvohConfig.keys[isAMS ? 'ams' : 'uhcm'][isProd ? 'prod' : 'dev'];
                if (envKeys) {
                    keys.writeKey = envKeys.writeKey || '';
                    keys.sourceKey = envKeys.sourceKey || '';
                }
            }
            
            if (isRvohConsumerEnabled && !isAgent) {
                console.log('[RvoHealth] Loading consumer integration script');
                !(function (co, h, e, s, i, o, n) {
                    var d = 'documentElement', a = 'className';
                    h[d][a] += ' preampjs fusejs';
                    n.k = e;
                    co._Cohesion = n;
                    co._Preamp = { k: s, start: new Date };
                    co._Fuse = { k: i };
                    co._Tagular = { k: o };
                    [e, s, i, o].map(function(x) {
                        co[x] = co[x] || function () {
                            (co[x].q = co[x].q || []).push([].slice.call(arguments))
                        }
                    });
                    h.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
                        co.setTimeout(function() {
                            var u = h[d][a]; h[d][a]=u.replace(/ ?preampjs| ?fusejs/g, '')
                        }, 3e3);
                        co._Preamp.docReady = co._Fuse.docReady = !0
                    });
                    var z = h.createElement('script');
                    z.async = 1;
                    z.src = 'https://cdn.rvohealth.com/cohesion/cohesion-to.min.js';
                    h.head.appendChild(z);
                    console.log('[RvoHealth] Consumer script loaded successfully');
                }
                (window, document, 'cohesion', 'preamp', 'fuse', 'tagular', {
                    tagular: {
                        writeKey: keys.writeKey,
                        sourceKey: keys.sourceKey,
                        taggy: { enabled: true }
                    }
                }));
            } else {
                console.log('[RvoHealth] Consumer integration skipped:', 
                    isAgent ? 'Agent flow detected' : 'Consumer flag disabled');
            }

            function loadAgentScript() {
                if (isRvohTelesalesEnabled && isAgent) {
                    console.log('[RvoHealth] Loading agent integration script');
                    sessionStorage.setItem('rvoh_id_found', isAgentAllowed ? 'true' : 'false');
                    
                    var style = document.createElement('style');
                    style.type = 'text/css';
                    style.textContent = ".preampjs [data-preamp], .fusejs [data-fuse] {opacity: 0 !important}";
                    document.head.appendChild(style);

                    var script = document.createElement('script');
                    script.async = true;
                    var agentEnv = isProd ? 'prod' : 'staging';
                    script.src = 'https://cohesion-scripts.rvohealth.dev/uhc-agent-' + agentEnv + '/index.js';
                    document.head.appendChild(script);
                    console.log('[RvoHealth] Agent script loaded from:', script.src);
                } else {
                    console.log('[RvoHealth] Agent integration skipped:',
                        !isRvohTelesalesEnabled ? 'Telesales flag disabled' : 'Not in agent flow');
                }
            }

            if (document.readyState !== 'loading') {
                loadAgentScript();
            } else {
                document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', loadAgentScript);
            }
        }
        
        initRvoHealth().catch(error => {
            console.log('[RvoHealth] Integration failed:', error);
        });
      } catch (e) {
            console.log('[RvoHealth] Integration error:', e);
      }
    })();
    </script>

<script>
    const currentEnvironment = (function () {
    const hostname = window.location.hostname;
        if (hostname.includes('qa')) return 'qa';
        if (hostname.includes('stage')) return 'stage';
        if (hostname.includes('dev') || hostname.includes('team') || hostname.includes('chargers')) return 'dev';
        return 'production';
    })();
    var medicareTxtHeader = location.href.split("/");
    var medicareText = medicareTxtHeader[3];
    if(medicareText && medicareText.indexOf('?') > -1){
        var medicareTextVal = medicareText.split('?');
        medicareText = medicareTextVal[0];
    }

    var language = 'en'; // Default to English
    if (window.location.hostname.includes('es-') || window.location.hostname.includes('es.')) {
        language = 'es'; // Set to Spanish if domain contains 'es-' or 'es.'
    }
    console.log('Detected language:', language);
    var environmentUrl = '';
    var esEnvironmentUrl = '';
    if (currentEnvironment === 'qa') {
        if(medicareText === 'medicare'){
            environmentUrl = 'https://uhc-qa.uhc.com';
            esEnvironmentUrl = 'https://es-uhc-stage.uhc.com/medicare';
        } else {
            environmentUrl = 'https://www.qa-aarpmedicareplans.uhc.com';
            esEnvironmentUrl = 'https://es-stage-aarpmedicareplans.uhc.com';
        }

    } else if (currentEnvironment === 'stage') {
        if(medicareText === 'medicare'){
            environmentUrl = 'https://uhc-stage.uhc.com';
            esEnvironmentUrl = 'https://es-uhc-stage.uhc.com/medicare';
        } else {
            environmentUrl = 'https://www.stage-aarpmedicareplans.uhc.com';
            esEnvironmentUrl = 'https://es-stage-aarpmedicareplans.uhc.com';
        }
    } else if (currentEnvironment === 'dev' || currentEnvironment === 'team') {
        if(medicareText === 'medicare'){
            environmentUrl = 'https://uhc-qa.uhc.com';
            esEnvironmentUrl = 'https://es-uhc-stage.uhc.com/medicare';
        } else {
            environmentUrl = 'https://www.chargers-aarpmedicareplans.uhc.com';
            esEnvironmentUrl = 'https://es-stage-aarpmedicareplans.uhc.com';
        }
    } else {
        if(medicareText === 'medicare'){
            environmentUrl = 'https://www.uhc.com/medicare';
            esEnvironmentUrl = 'https://es.uhc.com/medicare';
        } else {
            environmentUrl = 'https://www.aarpmedicareplans.com/';
            esEnvironmentUrl = 'https://es.aarpmedicareplans.com';
        }

    }
function getSpanishTranslations() {
    const flagsmithData = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('BULLET_TRAIN_DB') || '{}');
    if (flagsmithData && flagsmithData.flags) {
        const spanishTranslations = flagsmithData.flags.f1540343_spanish_translations;
        const isHomePage = location.pathname === '/' || location.pathname === '/medicare' || location.pathname === '/medicare/';
        const updateLangOptions = (path) => {
            if (typeof uhcStore !== 'undefined') {
                uhcStore.langOptions = [
                    {
                        href: language === 'es' ? environmentUrl + path : esEnvironmentUrl + path,
                        title: language === 'es' ? "English" : "Espaol",
                        lang: language === 'es' ? "en" : "es"
                    }
                ];
                const languageOptionsEvent = new CustomEvent("langOptions", { detail: uhcStore.langOptions });
                window.dispatchEvent(languageOptionsEvent);
            }
        };

        if (isHomePage && spanishTranslations.enabled === true) {
            console.log("Matched Home Page");
            updateLangOptions('/');
        } else if (spanishTranslations && spanishTranslations.enabled === true && spanishTranslations.value) {
            const translationPaths = spanishTranslations.value.split(',');
            for (let path of translationPaths) {
                if (location.pathname.includes(path.trim())) {
                    console.log("Matched:", path.trim());
                    updateLangOptions(location.pathname);
                    return;
                }
            }
            console.log("Not Matched");
        }
    }
    return null;
}

setTimeout(() => {
    getSpanishTranslations();
}, 4000);
</script>
